                  visibilityChange = "visibilitychange";             } else if (typeof document.mozHidden !== "undefined") {                   hidden = "mozHidden";                   visibilityChange = "mozvisibilitychange";             } else if (typeof document.msHidden !== "undefined") {                   hidden = "msHidden";                   visibilityChange = "msvisibilitychange";             } else if (typeof document.webkitHidden !== "undefined") {                   hidden = "webkitHidden";                   visibilityChange = "webkitvisibilitychange";             }                          // Core Features Logic             var loadFeatures = function() {                              }              // Event to be fired if BBOP is not displayed and page becomes visible             var handleVisibilityChange = function() {                 if (!document[hidden]) {                     // Only load BBOP once                     document.removeEventListener(visibilityChange, handleVisibilityChange);                     loadFeatures();                 }             }              if (typeof document.addEventListener === "undefined" ||                 typeof document[hidden] === "undefined" || !document[hidden]) {                 // If page is visible or visibility API unsupported, do BBOP now                 loadFeatures();             } else {                 // If page is not visible, listen for visibility change to display BBOP                 document.addEventListener(visibilityChange, handleVisibilityChange);             }         }); class="a-section"><div class="a-row a-spacing-micro"><div class="a-icon-row a-spacing-none"><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" title="5.0 out of 5 stars" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R21SEGZ4JLWRYT/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/187-3898119-0674836?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00B6SNAOI&nodeID=284507&store=kitchen"><i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5"></i></a><span class="a-letter-space"></span><a class="a-link-normal a-text-normal a-color-base" href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R21SEGZ4JLWRYT/ref=cm_cr_dp_title/187-3898119-0674836?ie=UTF8&ASIN=B00B6SNAOI&nodeID=284507&store=kitchen"><span class="a-size-base a-text-bold">Five Stars!</span></a></div><span class="a-color-secondary">         <span class="a-size-normal">     <span class="a-color-secondary">       By     </span>     <a href="/gp/pdp/profile/ABJQXRZXAD53U/ref=cm_cr_dp_pdp/187-3898119-0674836" class="noTextDecoration">maddie</a>   </span> <span class="a-color-secondary"> on November 19, 2014</span></span></div><div id="revData-dpReviewsMostHelpfulAUI-R21SEGZ4JLWRYT" class="a-row a-spacing-small"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold">     Verified Purchase   </span>      <div class="a-section">   These came super fast! I have a sister who.... Well let's just say this is right up her alley. :) For the most part, they look exactly like they do on the box. The brown on the little swirl could have been a little darker in my opinion, but the yellow on the droplet is super bright! Both of their faces are clear to see and you really can't help but smile when you see them. With one hole in the top of the swirl, five holes in the droplet, and soft plastic corks in the bottoms this is definitely a salt and pepper set to keep out on the table! </div>  </div>        <a
